<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черкнуть.html>черкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čerknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***подчинение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a> (8404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podčinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>submission, subjecting</li>
<li>subjection</li>
<li>subordination
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́нии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ v <b>podčinénii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">be subordinate; report</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ v <b>podčinénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">become subordinate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peredátʹ štó-libo v <b>podčinénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">place something under the authority</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́ча</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sdáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подчинить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a> (10238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">činítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subordinate <i>(to)</i>, to place (under), to place under the command</li>
<li>to subdue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>воле</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> svojéj vole</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bend to one's will</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> sebé</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to override</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dedicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> žiznʹ odnój céli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">dedicate one's life to one cause</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subordinate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиняться.html>подчиня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podčinjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиниться.html>подчини́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podčinítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подчинять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a> (19249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podčinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subordinate <i>(to)</i>, to place (under), to place under the command</li>
<li>to subdue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>воле</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> svojéj vole</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bend to one's will</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> sebé</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to override</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dedicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> žiznʹ odnój céli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">dedicate one's life to one cause</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subordinate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиняться.html>подчиня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podčinjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиниться.html>подчини́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podčinítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подшить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшить.html>подши́ть</a> (16344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшить.html>подши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podšítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подшива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hem</li>
<li>to sew on</li>
<li>to sew a sole on, to sole (a shoe)</li>
<li>to file (documents, etc.)</li></ol>

***подшутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшутить.html>подшути́ть</a> (25274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшутить.html>подшути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podšutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшучивать.html>подшу́чивать</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to laugh at, to mock, to make fun of</li>
<li>to play a joke on</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшучивать.html>подшу́чивать</a> (19272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшутить.html>подшути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podšutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшучивать.html>подшу́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podšúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшутить.html>подшути́ть</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to laugh at, to mock, to make fun of</li>
<li>to play a joke on</li></ol>

***подъезд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зд</a> (1755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Action noun from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podʺjéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to approach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjézd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́здов</a></b>)

***подъезжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a> (6755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive up (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>podʺjezžájet</b> k podʺjézdu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is driving up to the entrance</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ле</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móžno li <b>podʺjezžátʹ</b> sjudá na avtomobíle?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Can one drive a car here?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in, to pay a short visit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get (round), to start a pick up line, to get on the right side (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lóvko on k nej <b>podʺjezžájet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is getting round her very nicely; he is getting on the right side of her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подъем.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъем</a> (3113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднимать.html>поднима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The combining form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ём</span> is the normal deverbal equivalent of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">има́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare archaic first singular present tense <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">емлю́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jemljú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">има́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">подъём</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёмов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемный.html>подъёмный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lifting, raise, raising</li>
<li>hoisting <i>(of a flag)</i></li>
<li>salvaging <i>(of a sunken ship)</i></li>
<li>ascent, rise, upgrade</li>
<li>climb <i>(of a plane)</i></li>
<li>slope, rise <i>(of a mountain)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:величина.html>величина́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">veličiná <b>podʺjóma</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">up gradient</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>raising, development, upsurge</li>
<li>enthusiasm, animation</li>
<li>instep <i>(of a foot)</i></li>
<li>reveille</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> height (of vowels)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́днего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glásnyj srédnevo <b>podʺjóma</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mid vowel</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">vowel of middle height</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неподъемный.html>неподъёмный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepodʺjómnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podʺjómnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>подъёмные</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podʺjómnyje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***подъемник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a> (22046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подъём</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podʺjóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjómnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lift, elevator
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кузов.html>кузова</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самосвал.html>самосва́ла</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podʺjómnik</b> kuzova (u samosvála)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">body hoist</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> горнолыжников</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podʺjómnik</b> dlja gornolyžnikov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">ski lift</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подъехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a> (3926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive up (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>podʺjéxal</b> k podʺjézdu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He drove up to the entrance</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ле</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móžno li <b>podʺjéxatʹ</b> sjudá na avtomobíle?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Can one drive a car here?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in, to pay a short visit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get (round), to start a pick up line, to get on the right side (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хал</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lóvko on k nej <b>podʺjéxal</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He got round her very nicely; he got on the right side of her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подыграть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подыграть.html>подыгра́ть</a> (25409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подыграть.html>подыгра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podygrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подыгрывать.html>поды́грывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to accompany, to vamp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play into someone's hand</li>
<li>to play up <i>(to)</i></li></ol>
